shared_focus = {
	id = SGR_blankfocus
	icon = GFX_generic_support_the_left_right
	available = {
		always = no
	}
	bypass = {
	}
	offset = {
		x = 1
		y = 1
		trigger = {
			tag = SGR
		}
	}
	allow_branch = {
		has_country_flag = neverflag
	}
	cost = 2
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SGR_blankfocus"
	}
}

#Doppeldenken - Speer's reign of contrast begins.
shared_focus = {
	id = SGR_doppeldenken
	icon = GFX_GER_doppeldenken
	cost = 1.00
	x = 0
	y = 0

	allow_branch = {
		NOT = { has_global_flag = SGR_natsoc_collapse }
		NOT = {has_country_flag = SGR_phase2 }
		has_global_flag = german_civil_war_speervic
	}

	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SGR_doppeldenken"
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = speer.10004
				days = 130
				random = 60
			}
			country_event = {
				id = speer.10000
				days = 14
			}
			country_event = {
				id = speerflavor.104
				days = 4
			}
		}
	}
}

#In the Halls of Germania - the Gang of Four begins its energetic work in Germania's offices, planning for the future to come.
shared_focus = {
	id = SGR_in_the_halls_of_germania
	icon = GFX_GER_in_the_halls_of_germania
	cost = 1.00
	prerequisite = {
		focus = SGR_doppeldenken
	}
	relative_position_id = SGR_doppeldenken
	x = -1
	y = 1


	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SGR_in_the_halls_of_germania"
		add_political_power = 30
		custom_effect_tooltip = SGR_gang_of_four_work_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = speerflavor.32
				days = 17
			}
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		base = 20
		modifier = {
			NOT = {has_country_flag = SGR_created_RND}
			factor = 100
		}
	}
}

#On the Streets of Germany - Speer support reaches levels not seen before, with celebrations across Germany (atleast on the streets...)

		focus = SGR_doppeldenken
	}

	y = 1

			ideology = national_socialism
			popularity = -0.05
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		base = 20
		modifier = {
			NOT = {has_country_flag = SGR_created_RND}
			factor = 100
		}
	}
}

#Open the Ports - the Reich must trade with the outside world to sustain itself in these trying times.
shared_focus = {
	id = SGR_open_the_ports
	icon = GFX_GER_open_the_ports
	cost = 1.00
	prerequisite = {
		focus = SGR_aid_for_the_present
	}
	relative_position_id = SGR_aid_for_the_present
	x = 0
	y = 1



	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SGR_open_the_ports"
		custom_effect_tooltip = econ_increase_GDP_growth
		add_to_variable = {
			GDP_growth = 0.015
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_idea = tno_trade_laws_limited_exports } }
			add_ideas = tno_trade_laws_limited_exports
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		base = 20
		modifier = {
			NOT = {has_country_flag = SGR_created_RND}
			factor = 100
		}
	}
}

	cost = 1.00

		focus = SGR_suspend_the_persecution
	}
	relative_position_id = SGR_suspend_the_persecution
	x = -2
	y = 1



	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SGR_review_the_laws"
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = SGR_end_aryan_lineage_studies
			}
			add_political_power = 50
			else = {
				add_political_power = 20
			}
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		base = 20
		modifier = {
			NOT = {has_country_flag = SGR_created_RND}
			factor = 100
		}
	}
}

#Revitalizing Science - A large batch of investment into the Kaiser-Wilhelms-Gesellschaft, Fraunhofer Institut and other renomated German scientific agencies,
shared_focus = {
	id = SGR_revitalizing_science
	icon = GFX_GER_revitalizing_science
	cost = 1.00
	prerequisite = {
		focus = SGR_ausbildung_initiative
		focus = SGR_wehrmacht_engineering_schools
	}
	relative_position_id = SGR_wehrmacht_engineering_schools
	x = 1
	y = 1



	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SGR_revitalizing_science"
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = SGR_ausbildung_initiative
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				national_debt = 75
			}
			add_ideas = GER_SGR_scientific_investment
			TNO_improve_academic_base_high = yes
			TNO_improve_research_facilities_med = yes
			else = {
				add_to_variable = {
					national_debt = 75
				}
				add_ideas = GER_SGR_scientific_investment
				TNO_improve_academic_base_med = yes
				TNO_improve_research_facilities_low = yes
			}
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		base = 20
		modifier = {
			has_country_flag = SGR_created_RND
			factor = 100
		}
	}
}

#Inflation Control - The money supply is being decreased with contractionary monetary policy, leading to an immediate decrease in both GDP and debt.
shared_focus = {
	id = SGR_inflation_control
	icon = GFX_GER_inflation_control
	cost = 1.00
	prerequisite = {
		focus = SGR_wahrungsreform
	}
	mutually_exclusive = {
		focus = SGR_price_deregulation
	}
	relative_position_id = SGR_wahrungsreform
	x = -1
	y = 1



	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SGR_inflation_control"
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_political_power = -30
		add_to_variable = { national_debt = 50 }
		add_to_variable = { GDP = -50 }
		TNO_worsen_poverty_low = yes
		
		increase_wwgrowth_small = yes
		decrease_regime_stab_small = yes

shared_focus = {
	id = GER_back_into_the_pakt
	icon = GFX_GER_Pakt_Wargames
	prerequisite = {
		focus = GER_architects_of_the_nation
	}
	prerequisite = {
		focus = GER_rescind_occupation_laws
	}

	relative_position_id = GER_architects_of_the_nation
	x = -1
	y = 1

	cost = 1

	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus GER_back_into_the_pakt"
		if = {
			limit = { NOR = { has_government = despotism } }
			add_to_faction = NOR
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { NOR = { has_government = fascism } }
			NOR = { save_party_popularities = yes }
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_dlc = "Together for Victory"
						has_dlc = "Man the Guns"
					}
				}
				set_autonomy = {
					target = NOR
					autonomy_state = autonomy_collaborator_puppet_state
				}
			}
			else = { puppet = NOR }
			NOR = { apply_party_popularities = yes }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { NOR = { has_government = national_socialism } }
			NOR = { save_party_popularities = yes }
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_dlc = "Together for Victory"
						has_dlc = "Man the Guns"
					}
				}
				set_autonomy = {
					target = NOR
					autonomy_state = autonomy_collaborator_puppet_state
				}
			}
			else = { puppet = NOR }
			hidden_effect = {
				NOR = {
					apply_party_popularities = yes
					set_politics = { ruling_party = national_socialism }
				}
			}
		}
		NOR = {join_zollverein = yes}
	}
}

					}

						target = AZR
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}			
			if = {
				limit = {
					GEO = {
						owns_state = 231
						}
					}
					declare_war_on = {
						target = GEO
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}			
			if = {
				limit = {
					ADY = {
						owns_state = 233
						}
					}
					declare_war_on = {
						target = ADY
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}			
			if = {
				limit = {
					DAG = {
						owns_state = 232
						}
					}
					declare_war_on = {
						target = DAG
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
			}
	}
}

				target = JAP
				modifier = embargo
			}
			JAP = {
				remove_opinion_modifier = {
					target = GER
					modifier = TNO_embargo
				}
			}
			JAP = {
				remove_opinion_modifier = {
					target = GER
					modifier = embargo
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SGR_JAP_major_speerjapan_GER_manchuko_the_forge
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = speerjapan_tariffs_large

					has_country_flag = speerjapan_tariffs_small

shared_focus = {
	id = GER_we_the_buyer
	icon = GFX_ANG_pay_them_well
	cost = 1.00
	relative_position_id = GER_japan_the_supplier
	x = 0
	y = 1
	prerequisite = { focus = GER_japan_the_supplier }
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus GER_we_the_buyer"
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = speerjapan_tariffs_small }
			add_to_variable = {
				misc_costs = 50
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SGR_JAP_major_speerjapan_tariffs_small
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = speerjapan_tariffs_medium }
			add_to_variable = {
				misc_costs = 30
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SGR_JAP_major_speerjapan_tariffs_medium
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = speerjapan_tariffs_large }
			add_to_variable = {
				misc_costs = 10
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SGR_JAP_major_speerjapan_tariffs_large
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = speerjapan_tariffs_large
					has_country_flag = speerjapan_tariffs_medium
					has_country_flag = speerjapan_tariffs_small
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SGR_JAP_major_waiting_for_negotiation
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = speerjapan_finished_tech_treaty
					has_country_flag = speerjapan_finished_noninvolvement_treaty
					has_country_flag = speerjapan_finished_investment_treaty
					has_country_flag = speerjapan_finished_tariff_treaty
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = speerjapan_number_of_sucessful_negotiations
						value = 4
						compare = equals
					}
				}
				news_event = { id = WORLD.2052 days = 1 }
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							var = speerjapan_number_of_sucessful_negotiations
							value = 3
							compare = equals
						}
					}
					news_event = { id = WORLD.2052 days = 1 } 
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							var = speerjapan_number_of_sucessful_negotiations
							value = 2
							compare = equals
						}
					}
					news_event = { id = WORLD.2053 days = 1 } 
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							var = speerjapan_number_of_sucessful_negotiations
							value = 1
							compare = equals
						}
					}
					news_event = { id = WORLD.2053 days = 1 } 
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							var = speerjapan_number_of_sucessful_negotiations
							value = 0
							compare = equals
						}
					}
					news_event = { id = WORLD.2054 days = 1 } 
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	available = {
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = SGR_tooltip_the_masters_of_europe
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = speerjapan_technology_small
				has_country_flag = speerjapan_technology_medium
				has_country_flag = speerjapan_technology_large
			}
		}
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus GER_the_masters_of_europe"
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = speerjapan_technology_small }
			army_experience = 10
			}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = speerjapan_technology_medium }
			army_experience = 10
			add_tech_bonus = {
				bonus = 0.5
				uses = 2
				category = land_doctrine
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = speerjapan_technology_large }
			add_tech_bonus = {
				bonus = 1
				uses = 2
				category = land_doctrine
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = speerjapan_technology_large
					has_country_flag = speerjapan_technology_medium
					has_country_flag = speerjapan_technology_small
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SGR_JAP_major_waiting_for_negotiation
		}
	}
}

shared_focus = {
	id = GER_the_army_of_barons
	icon = GFX_generic_nazi_jet_2
	cost = 1.00
	relative_position_id = GER_the_kings_of_the_atlantic
	x = 0
	y = 1
	prerequisite = { focus = GER_the_kings_of_the_atlantic }
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus GER_the_army_of_barons"
			if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = speerjapan_technology_small }
			add_tech_bonus = {
				bonus = 0.5
				uses = 1
				category = radar_tech
				}
			}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = speerjapan_technology_medium }
			add_tech_bonus = {
				bonus = 0.5
				uses = 1
				category = radar_tech
			}
			add_tech_bonus = {
				bonus = 1
				uses = 2
				category = air_equipment
			}
			add_tech_bonus = {
				bonus = 1
				uses = 2
				category = air_doctrine
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = speerjapan_technology_large }
			add_tech_bonus = {
				bonus = 0.5
				uses = 1
				category = radar_tech
			}
			add_tech_bonus = {
				bonus = 1
				uses = 2
				category = air_equipment
			}
			add_tech_bonus = {
				bonus = 1
				uses = 2
				category = air_doctrine
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = speerjapan_technology_large
					has_country_flag = speerjapan_technology_medium
					has_country_flag = speerjapan_technology_small
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SGR_JAP_major_waiting_for_negotiation
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = speerjapan_finished_tech_treaty
					has_country_flag = speerjapan_finished_noninvolvement_treaty
					has_country_flag = speerjapan_finished_investment_treaty
					has_country_flag = speerjapan_finished_tariff_treaty
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = speerjapan_number_of_sucessful_negotiations
						value = 4
						compare = equals
					}
				}
				news_event = { id = WORLD.2052 days = 1 }
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							var = speerjapan_number_of_sucessful_negotiations
							value = 3
							compare = equals
						}
					}
					news_event = { id = WORLD.2052 days = 1 } 
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							var = speerjapan_number_of_sucessful_negotiations
							value = 2
							compare = equals
						}
					}
					news_event = { id = WORLD.2053 days = 1 } 
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							var = speerjapan_number_of_sucessful_negotiations
							value = 1
							compare = equals
						}
					}
					news_event = { id = WORLD.2053 days = 1 } 
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							var = speerjapan_number_of_sucessful_negotiations
							value = 0
							compare = equals
						}
					}
					news_event = { id = WORLD.2054 days = 1 } 
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

				subtract_from_variable = {ZollvereinPayments = 0.05}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FRA = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
			}

	id = SGR_ein_fuhrer
	icon = GFX_GER_Ein_Fuhrer_2
	cost = 3.00

	prerequisite = {
		focus = SGR_ein_volk
	}
	prerequisite = {
		focus = SGR_ein_reich
	}

	relative_position_id = SGR_ein_reich
	x = -1
	y = 1

	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SGR_ein_fuhrer"
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_SGR_statereich_end_tt
		country_event = {
			id = speerphase3.6
			days = 2
		}
		set_country_flag = SGR_state_reich_disable
		custom_effect_tooltip = SGRPhase3FashEinFuhrer
	}
}

#AUTHDEM SPEER BRANCH

#The Dream Come True (Authdem) - Speer has lost his power, bullied to the brink by the Gang of Four. They're now the new power behind the throne, and Speer is their puppet.
shared_focus = {
	id = SGR_the_dream_come_true_auth
	icon = GFX_GER_democracy_vic
	cost = 3.00

	allow_branch = {
		has_country_flag = SGR_SR_authdem_outcome
	}

	prerequisite = {
		focus = SGR_the_sword_has_fallen
	}

	relative_position_id = SGR_the_sword_has_fallen
	x = 0
	y = 1

	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SGR_the_dream_come_true_auth"
		country_event = {
			id = speerphase3.7
			days = 2
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_mission = SGR_Regime_Collapse_Impeding
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SGRPhase3AuthdemTheDreamComeTrue
	}
}

#The House of Cards Falls - The NSDAP is the final obstacle towards democratization of Germany, and it is already crumbling at the sight of what happened. Time to accelerate it.
shared_focus = {
	id = SGR_the_house_of_cards_falls
	icon = GFX_Generic_Admininistration
	cost = 3.00

	prerequisite = {
		focus = SGR_the_dream_come_true_auth
	}

	relative_position_id = SGR_the_dream_come_true_auth
	x = -1
	y = 1

	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SGR_the_house_of_cards_falls"
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = -0.1 
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_socialism
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		add_political_power = 50
		custom_effect_tooltip = SGRPhase3AuthdemTheHouseOfCards
	}
}

#The Shadow Government - The Gang of Four is now in a position to call itself the new shadow government of Germany. It is time to collect all contacts available to them and establish themselves truly as such.
shared_focus = {
	id = SGR_the_shadow_government
	icon = GFX_GER_on_the_streets_of_germania
	cost = 3.00

	prerequisite = {
		focus = SGR_the_dream_come_true_auth
	}

	relative_position_id = SGR_the_dream_come_true_auth
	x = 1
	y = 1

	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SGR_the_shadow_government"
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = GER_SGR_gang_of_four
			add_idea = GER_SGR_shadow_government
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SGRPhase3AuthdemTheShadowGovernment
	}
}

#Contact Popular Movements - even before the Slave Revolt, new movements established themselves across Germany in protest against the Nazi government. Striking up contact to them is an excellent way to further pluralize the German political scene and disrupt NSDAP unity.
shared_focus = {
	id = SGR_contact_popular_movements
	icon = GFX_GER_Contact_Popular_Movements
	cost = 3.00

	prerequisite = {
		focus = SGR_the_shadow_government
	}
	prerequisite = {
		focus = SGR_the_house_of_cards_falls
	}

	relative_position_id = SGR_the_house_of_cards_falls
	x = 1
	y = 1

	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SGR_contact_popular_movements"
		country_event = {
			id = speerphase3.8
			days = 2
		}
		increase_reformist_leaning_large = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = SGRPhase3AuthdemContactPopularMovements
	}
}

#Einigkeit - The German people need unity, and what unifies them the most right now is their collective dissatisfaction with the NSDAP. It is time to bank on this.

	cost = 3.00

	prerequisite = {
		focus = SGR_contact_popular_movements
	}

	relative_position_id = SGR_contact_popular_movements
	x = -1
	y = 1

	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SGR_einigkeit"
		add_regime_stab_med = yes
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SGRPhase3AuthdemEinigkeit
	}
}

#Recht - The Reich has been plagued by illegal 'special' trials since the beginning of the Nazi regime. It is time for one last such trial - the one to end all of them...
shared_focus = {
	id = SGR_recht
	icon = GFX_GER_justice
	cost = 3.00

	prerequisite = {
		focus = SGR_contact_popular_movements
	}

	relative_position_id = SGR_contact_popular_movements
	x = 1
	y = 1

	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SGR_recht"
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_SGR_recht_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			GER = {
				drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
				set_cosmetic_tag = SGR_authdem2
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = SGR_reichslander
				}
				country_event = {
					id = speerphase3.9
					days = 2
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#KN SUBTREE

#A New Era - recent events have shown us that the world cannot stay divided. Regardless of our ideological standpoint, we must embrace global diplomacy to avoid letting this happen again.
shared_focus = {
	id = SGR_a_new_era
	icon = GFX_GER_germanian_cherry_blossoms
	cost = 3.00

	allow_branch = {
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = SGR_SR_fash_outcome
			has_country_flag = SGR_SR_authdem_outcome
		}
	}

	prerequisite = {
		focus = SGR_reichsschutzgruppe
	}
	prerequisite = {
		focus = SGR_the_plan_going_forward
	}
	prerequisite = {
		focus = SGR_freiheit
		focus = SGR_ein_fuhrer
	}

	relative_position_id = SGR_reichsschutzgruppe
	x = 4
	y = 1

	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SGR_a_new_era"
		country_event = {
			id = speerphase3.11
			days = 2
		}
		add_regime_stab_small = yes
	}
}

#Prime the Ambassadors - Soon, there will be another run for international diplomacy. It is time to prepare for it, and we can do this best by preparing our embassies across the world.
shared_focus = {
	id = SGR_prime_the_ambassadors
	icon = GFX_GER_a_bureaucracy_to_rely_on
	cost = 3.00

	prerequisite = {
		focus = SGR_a_hint_in_the_east
	}
	prerequisite = {
		focus = SGR_time_for_change
	}
	prerequisite = {
		focus = SGR_an_example_in_the_west
	}


	relative_position_id = SGR_time_for_change
	x = -1
	y = 1

	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SGR_prime_the_ambassadors"
		USA = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = GER
				modifier = GER_ambassadors_primed
			}
		}
		JAP = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = GER
				modifier = GER_ambassadors_primed
			}
		}
	}
}

#Koalition der Nationen - the letters have been drafted and are being sent out into the world.
shared_focus = {
	id = SGR_koalition_der_nationen
	icon = GFX_GER_koalition_der_nationen
	cost = 3.00

	prerequisite = {
		focus = SGR_collect_the_proposals
	}
	prerequisite = {
		focus = SGR_prime_the_ambassadors
	}


	relative_position_id = SGR_prime_the_ambassadors
	x = 1
	y = 2

	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SGR_koalition_der_nationen"
		custom_effect_tooltip = SGR_KN_focus_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			JAP = {
				country_event = {
					id = speerphase3.14
					days = 2
				}
			}
			USA = {
				country_event = {
					id = speerphase3.14
					days = 2
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SGR_ein_fuhrer
				}
				country_event = {
					id = speerphase3.15
					days = 4
				}
				else = {
					country_event = {
						id = speerphase3.16
						days = 4
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Germany's Speer path is the product of a team getting together, openly discussing and sharing their thoughts. It was an iterative process over the course of almost a year - and we hope that you've
# enjoyed a small peak into a world that, whilst dark and looming, still has some glimmers of hope that may grow into a fire. Thank you so much for playing, and we hope you'll come back for the rest
# of Speer's and the Gang of Four's story in TNO2!
